<h2 class='one'>G'Day!</h2>
<h2 class='two hide'>Please Sign In</h2>
<p>
<span class='fs-desc1'>Favstar gets even better if you sign in.</span>
</p>
<p class='fs-btn-sign-in'>

</p>
<p class='fs-heres-why'>
<a class='fs-more-info'>
<span>Here's why</span>
signing in is good for you.
</a>
</p>
<img class='fs-arrow' src='http://assets0.favster.fm/assets/meta/sign_in_arrow-7e8bfadd762033402a65d04b01058f8651503a4ded564596dbfc6458ce294821.png'>

</li>
<li class='fs-last hide' id='meta_sign_in_more'>
<div class='row-fluid'>
<div class='fs span6'>
<ul>
<li>
You get a personalized view of Favstar based on the people you follow.
</li>
<li>
Your likes and retweets are collected instantly, meaning your status and stats get updated at blazing speeds.
</li>
<li>
Use lists to manage your friends, and keep on top of where the fav-love is happening.
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class='fs span6'>
<h3>Your account is safe, of course!</h3>
<ul>
<li>
We never see your twitter password.
</li>
<li>
We won't tweet or follow anyone without your permission.
</li>
<li>
We only use your API calls when you like, retweet, or follow someone.
</li>
</ul>
</div>
